  \ progression modeling and then discusses staging from cross-sectional data and\
  \ simultaneous staging and subtyping.</p>\r\n<p>Speaker: David Sontag</p>\r\n  \

  <span m="710920">should</span> <span m="711100">first</span> <span m="711550">start</span>
  <span m="712120">by</span> <span m="712420">working</span> <span m="712780">with</span>
  <span m="713020">either</span> <span m="713290">synthetic</span> <span m="714070">data,</span>
  <span m="714940">or</span> <span m="715070">we should</span> <span m="715190">start</span>
  <span m="715450">with</span> <span m="715600">working</span> <span m="715930">with</span>
  <span m="716110">a</span> <span m="716140">disease</span> <span m="716770">where</span>
  <span m="717100">we</span> <span m="717280">have</span> <span m="717490">some</span>
  <span m="717880">idea</span> <span m="718420">of</span> <span m="718510">what</span>
  <span m="718720">the</span> <span m="718810">actual</span> <span m="719260">true</span>
  <span m="719520">disease</span> <span m="719800">staging</span> <span m="720280">is.</span>
  <span m="721180">And</span> <span m="721360">that</span> <span m="721540">way,</span>
  <span m="721690">we</span> <span m="721810">can</span> <span m="721960">look</span>
  <span m="722080">to</span> <span m="722230">see</span> <span m="722500">what</span>
  <span m="722680">our</span> <span m="722800">algorithms</span> <span m="723340">would</span>
  <span m="723520">recover</span> <span m="724150">in</span> <span m="724270">those</span>
  <span m="724420">scenarios,</span> <span m="724970">and</span> <span m="725070">does</span>
  <span m="725110">it</span> <span m="725800">align</span> <span m="726280">with</span>
  <span m="726520">what</span> <span m="726760">we</span> <span m="726880">would</span>
  <span m="727000">expect</span> <span m="728110">either</span> <span m="728410">from</span>
  <span m="728830">the</span> <span m="728950">way</span> <span m="729100">the</span>
  <span m="729190">data</span> <span m="729400">was</span> <span m="729460">generated</span>
  <span m="730030">or</span> <span m="730180">from</span> <span m="730620">the</span>
  <span m="730720">existing</span> <span m="731080">medical</span> <span m="731380">literature.</span></p><p><span
  m="732810">And</span> <span m="732910">that's</span> <span m="733120">why</span>
  <span m="733240">we</span> <span m="733330">chose</span> <span m="733540">COPD.</span>
  <span m="734170">Because</span> <span m="734410">it</span> <span m="734470">is</span>
  <span m="734560">well-understood,</span> <span m="736780">and</span> <span m="737000">there's</span>
  <span m="737200">a</span> <span m="737230">wealth</span> <span m="737530">of</span>
  <span m="737590">literature</span> <span m="737950">on</span> <span m="738100">it,</span>
  <span m="739300">and</span> <span m="739840">because</span> <span m="740320">we</span>
  <span m="740440">have</span> <span m="740620">data</span> <span m="740950">on</span>
  <span m="741160">it</span> <span m="741670">which</span> <span m="741910">is</span>
  <span m="742030">much</span> <span m="742390">messier</span> <span m="742930">than</span>
  <span m="743050">the</span> <span m="743140">type</span> <span m="743380">of</span>
  <span m="743470">data</span> <span m="743650">that</span> <span m="743770">went</span>
  <span m="744010">into</span> <span m="744190">the</span> <span m="744280">original</span>
  <span m="744580">studies,</span> <span m="745330">and</span> <span m="745540">we</span>
  <span m="745630">could</span> <span m="745750">ask,</span> <span m="746050">could</span>
  <span m="746260">we</span> <span m="746350">come</span> <span m="746530">to</span>
  <span m="746620">the</span> <span m="746710">same</span> <span m="746890">conclusions</span>
  <span m="747580">as</span> <span m="747730">those</span> <span m="747910">original</span>
  <span m="748240">studies?</span></p><p><span m="755180">So</span> <span m="756230">in</span>
  <span m="756440">this</span> <span m="756680">work,</span> <span m="757400">we're</span>
  <span m="757580">going</span> <span m="757850">to</span> <span m="757970">use</span>
  <span m="758240">data</span> <span m="758540">from</span> <span m="759110">the</span>
  <span m="759230">electronic</span> <span m="759710">medical</span> <span m="760010">record.</span>
  <span m="761860">We're</span> <span m="762040">only</span> <span m="762250">going</span>
  <span m="762350">to</span> <span m="762430">look</span> <span m="762700">at</span>
  <span m="763390">a</span> <span m="763450">subset</span> <span m="763930">of</span>
  <span m="764020">the</span> <span m="764110">EMR,</span> <span m="764500">in</span>
  <span m="764590">particular,</span> <span m="765400">diagnosis</span> <span m="766180">codes</span>
  <span m="766960">that</span> <span m="767200">are</span> <span m="767260">recorded</span>
  <span m="767680">for a</span> <span m="767800">patient</span> <span m="768100">at</span>
  <span m="768160">any</span> <span m="768450">point</span> <span m="768850">in</span>
  <span m="768970">time,</span> <span m="770300">and</span> <span m="770320">we're</span>
  <span m="770440">going</span> <span m="770680">to</span> <span m="770830">assume</span>
  <span m="771160">that</span> <span m="771250">we</span> <span m="771370">do</span>
  <span m="771520">not</span> <span m="771850">have</span> <span m="772090">access</span>
  <span m="772390">to</span> <span m="772480">spirometry</span> <span m="773050">data</span>
  <span m="773320">at</span> <span m="773410">all.</span> <span m="773800">So</span>
  <span m="774010">we</span> <span m="774130">don't</span> <span m="774610">have</span>
  <span m="775060">any</span> <span m="775690">obvious</span> <span m="776200">way</span>
  <span m="776380">of</span> <span m="776500">staging</span> <span m="777010">the</span>
  <span m="777100">patient's</span> <span m="777490">disease.</span> <span m="780490">The</span>
  <span m="780580">general</span> <span m="780880">approach</span> <span m="781210">is</span>
  <span m="781330">going</span> <span m="781540">to</span> <span m="781660">be</span>
  <span m="781870">to</span> <span m="782080">build</span> <span m="783670">a</span>
  <span m="784090">generative</span> <span m="784840">model</span> <span m="785560">for</span>
  <span m="785950">disease</span> <span m="786340">progression.</span></p><p><span
  m="789840">At</span> <span m="789960">a</span> <span m="789990">very</span> <span
  m="790200">high</span> <span m="790380">level,</span> <span m="790930">this</span>
  <span m="791430">is</span> <span m="791940">a</span> <span m="792210">Markov</span>
  <span m="792750">model.</span> <span m="793290">It's</span> <span m="793440">a</span>
  <span m="793470">model</span> <span m="793890">that</span> <span m="794430">specifies</span>
  <span m="795600">the</span> <span m="796590">distribution</span> <span m="797580">of</span>
  <span m="798630">the</span> <span m="798870">patient's</span> <span m="799380">data,</span>
  <span m="799860">which</span> <span m="800040">is</span> <span m="800160">shown</span>
  <span m="800400">here</span> <span m="800550">in</span> <span m="800640">the</span>
  <span m="800700">bottom,</span> <span m="801600">as</span> <span m="801990">it</span>
  <span m="802230">evolves</span> <span m="802830">over</span> <span m="803100">time.</span>
  <span m="805750">According</span> <span m="806320">to a</span> <span m="806530">number</span>
  <span m="806860">of</span> <span m="806980">hidden</span> <span m="807370">variables</span>
  <span m="808180">that</span> <span m="808360">are</span> <span m="808450">shown</span>
  <span m="808720">in</span> <span m="808780">the</span> <span m="808870">top,</span>
  <span m="809350">these</span> <span m="809590">S</span> <span m="809920">variables</span>
  <span m="810430">that</span> <span m="810550">denote</span> <span m="810850">disease</span>
  <span m="811150">stages,</span> <span m="811840">and</span> <span m="811930">these</span>
  <span m="812140">X</span> <span m="812440">variables</span> <span m="812860">that</span>
  <span m="812980">denote</span> <span m="813880">comorbidities</span> <span m="814590">that</span>
  <span m="814660">the</span> <span m="814720">patient</span> <span m="814990">might</span>
  <span m="815140">have</span> <span m="815530">at</span> <span m="815680">that</span>
  <span m="815920">point</span> <span m="816220">in</span> <span m="816310">time,</span>
  <span m="818380">these</span> <span m="818520">X</span> <span m="818910">and</span>
  <span m="819060">S</span> <span m="819240">variables</span> <span m="819780">are</span>
  <span m="819870">always</span> <span m="820170">assumed</span> <span m="820530">to</span>
  <span m="820620">the</span> <span m="820770">unobserved.</span> <span m="821550">So</span>
  <span m="821910">if</span> <span m="822030">you</span> <span m="822130">were</span>
  <span m="822170">to</span> <span m="822270">clump</span> <span m="822660">them</span>
  <span m="822810">together</span> <span m="823200">into</span> <span m="823380">one</span>
  <span m="823560">variable,</span> <span m="824040">this</span> <span m="824190">would</span>
  <span m="824310">look</span> <span m="824520">exactly</span> <span m="824940">like</span>
  <span m="825120">a</span> <span m="825180">hidden</span> <span m="825450">Markov</span>
  <span m="825780">model.</span></p><p><span m="827860">And</span> <span m="827980">moreover,</span>
  <span m="829210">we're</span> <span m="829600">not</span> <span m="829960">going</span>
  <span m="830200">to</span> <span m="830350">assume</span> <span m="830800">that</span>
  <span m="830980">we</span> <span m="831130">have</span> <span m="831700">a</span>
  <span m="831760">lot</span> <span m="832090">of</span> <span m="832240">longitudinal</span>
  <span m="832960">data</span> <span m="833320">for</span> <span m="833470">a</span>
  <span m="833560">patient.</span> <span m="834520">In</span> <span m="834610">particular,</span>
  <span m="835390">COPD</span> <span m="835990">evolves</span> <span m="836530">over</span>
  <span m="836680">a</span> <span m="836710">10</span> <span m="837040">to</span>
  <span m="837160">20</span> <span m="837580">years,</span> <span m="838300">and</span>
  <span m="838420">the</span> <span m="838480">data</span> <span m="838720">that</span>
  <span m="838870">we'll</span> <span m="838990">be</span> <span m="839080">learning</span>
  <span m="839350">from</span> <span m="839560">here</span> <span m="840130">has</span>
  <span m="840340">data</span> <span m="840670">only</span> <span m="841270">over</span>
  <span m="841810">one</span> <span m="842140">to</span> <span m="842260">three-year</span>
  <span m="842860">time</span> <span m="843130">range.</span> <span m="844360">The</span>
  <span m="844450">challenge</span> <span m="845290">will</span> <span m="845470">be,</span>
  <span m="845680">can</span> <span m="845920">we</span> <span m="846040">take</span>
  <span m="846370">data</span> <span m="847750">in</span> <span m="847850">this</span>
  <span m="847990">one</span> <span m="848200">to</span> <span m="848290">three-year</span>
  <span m="849250">time</span> <span m="849550">range</span> <span m="850510">and</span>
  <span m="850630">somehow</span> <span m="850930">stitch</span> <span m="851330">it</span>
  <span m="851440">together</span> <span m="851980">across</span> <span m="852340">large</span>
  <span m="852610">numbers</span> <span m="852880">of</span> <span m="852940">patients</span>
  <span m="853330">to</span> <span m="853450">get</span> <span m="853600">a</span>
  <span m="853660">picture</span> <span m="854020">of</span> <span m="854110">what</span>
  <span m="854260">the</span> <span m="854350">20-year</span> <span m="854800">progression</span>
  <span m="855250">of the</span> <span m="855340">disease</span> <span m="855580">might</span>
  <span m="855760">look</span> <span m="856000">like?</span> <span m="857500">The</span>
  <span m="857590">way</span> <span m="857740">that</span> <span m="857860">we're</span>
  <span m="857950">going</span> <span m="858130">to</span> <span m="858250">do</span>
  <span m="858490">that</span> <span m="858790">is</span> <span m="858940">by</span>
  <span m="859120">learning</span> <span m="859660">the</span> <span m="859810">parameters</span>
  <span m="860590">of</span> <span m="860710">this</span> <span m="860860">probabilistic</span>
  <span m="861370">model.</span> <span m="862640">And</span> <span m="862740">then</span>
  <span m="862750">from</span> <span m="862990">the</span> <span m="863050">parameters,</span>
  <span m="863740">we're</span> <span m="863830">going</span> <span m="864070">to</span>
  <span m="864280">either</span> <span m="865060">infer</span> <span m="865750">the</span>
  <span m="865870">patient's</span> <span m="866320">actual</span> <span m="866680">disease</span>
  <span m="866920">stage</span> <span m="867310">and</span> <span m="867460">thus</span>
  <span m="867670">sort</span> <span m="867970">them,</span> <span m="868660">or</span>
  <span m="868840">actually</span> <span m="869080">simulate</span> <span m="870400">data</span>

  <span m="871720">to</span> <span m="871810">see</span> <span m="872020">what</span>
  <span m="872170">a</span> <span m="872230">20-year</span> <span m="872770">trajectory</span>
  <span m="873190">might</span> <span m="873370">look</span> <span m="873580">like.</span>
  <span m="875180">Is</span> <span m="875300">the</span> <span m="875390">goal</span>
  <span m="875600">clear?</span></p><p><span m="878900">All</span> <span m="878980">right.</span>
  <span m="879160">So</span> <span m="879280">now</span> <span m="879430">what</span>
  <span m="879550">I'm</span> <span m="879640">going</span> <span m="879790">to</span>
  <span m="879910">do</span> <span m="880000">is</span> <span m="880090">I'm</span>
  <span m="880180">going</span> <span m="880420">to</span> <span m="880540">step</span>
  <span m="881620">into</span> <span m="882100">this</span> <span m="882310">model</span>

  <span m="885730">and</span> <span m="885850">I'll</span> <span m="885910">start</span>
  <span m="886180">out</span> <span m="886300">with</span> <span m="886480">a</span>

  <span m="889570">the</span> <span m="889660">red</span> <span m="889850">box.</span>
  <span m="891790">So</span> <span m="891970">this</span> <span m="892330">is</span>
  <span m="892630">the</span> <span m="892810">model</span> <span m="893320">of</span>
  <span m="893440">the</span> <span m="893620">patient's</span> <span m="894220">disease</span>
  <span m="894730">progression</span> <span m="896280">at</span> <span m="896430">any</span>
  <span m="896640">one</span> <span m="896820">point</span> <span m="897030">in</span>
  <span m="897120">time.</span> <span m="898060">So</span> <span m="898440">this</span>
  <span m="898710">variable,</span> <span m="899160">S1,</span> <span m="899640">for</span>
  <span m="899790">example,</span> <span m="900180">might</span> <span m="900390">denote</span>
  <span m="900690">the</span> <span m="900780">patient's</span> <span m="901170">disease</span>

  <span m="905460">2011;</span> <span m="906810">S2</span> <span m="907170">might</span>
  <span m="907410">denote</span> <span m="907650">the</span> <span m="907710">patient's</span>
  <span m="908010">disease</span> <span m="908250">stage</span> <span m="908850">April</span>
  <span m="909150">2011;</span> <span m="910470">S</span> <span m="910680">capital</span>

  <span m="911760">the</span> <span m="911820">patient's</span> <span m="912120">disease</span>
  <span m="912390">stage</span> <span m="912870">June</span> <span m="913260">2012.</span>
  <span m="914850">So</span> <span m="915000">we're</span> <span m="915090">going</span>
  <span m="915300">to</span> <span m="915450">have</span> <span m="916140">one</span>
  <span m="916710">random</span> <span m="917100">variable</span> <span m="918420">for</span>
  <span m="918810">each</span> <span m="919260">observation</span> <span m="920760">of</span>
  <span m="921060">the</span> <span m="921180">patient's</span> <span m="921630">data</span>
  <span m="921900">that</span> <span m="922020">we</span> <span m="922110">have.</span>
  <span m="922860">And</span> <span m="922950">notice</span> <span m="923280">that</span>
  <span m="923400">the</span> <span m="923490">observations</span> <span m="924150">of</span>
  <span m="924210">the</span> <span m="924270">patient's</span> <span m="924600">data</span>
  <span m="924870">might</span> <span m="925140">be</span> <span m="925260">at</span>
  <span m="925350">very</span> <span m="925650">irregular</span> <span m="926280">time</span>
  <span m="926580">intervals,</span> <span m="927610">and</span> <span m="927810">that's</span>
  <span m="928050">going</span> <span m="928230">to</span> <span m="928320">be</span>
  <span m="928410">OK</span> <span m="928740">with</span> <span m="928890">this</span>
  <span m="929010">approach,</span> <span m="930020">OK?</span> <span m="930240">So</span>
  <span m="930630">notice</span> <span m="930960">that</span> <span m="931110">there</span>
  <span m="931180">is</span> <span m="931350">a</span> <span m="932040">one-month</span>

  <span m="933750">and</span> <span m="933840">S2,</span> <span m="934830">but</span>
  <span m="935100">a</span> <span m="937990">four-month</span> <span m="938770">gap</span>

  <span m="941950">OK?</span> <span m="942220">So</span> <span m="942430">we're</span>
  <span m="942520">going</span> <span m="942700">to</span> <span m="942790">model</span>
  <span m="943120">the</span> <span m="943210">patient's</span> <span m="943540">disease</span>
  <span m="943870">stage</span> <span m="944350">at</span> <span m="944620">the</span>
  <span m="944740">point</span> <span m="944950">in</span> <span m="945040">time</span>
  <span m="945250">when</span> <span m="945370">we</span> <span m="945460">have</span>
  <span m="945670">an</span> <span m="945790">observation</span> <span m="946450">for</span>
  <span m="946660">the</span> <span m="946750">patient.</span></p><p><span m="949510">S</span>
  <span m="950590">denotes</span> <span m="951160">a</span> <span m="951490">discrete</span>
  <span m="952540">disease</span> <span m="952960">stage</span> <span m="953620">in</span>
  <span m="953770">this</span> <span m="954250">model.</span> <span m="954820">So</span>
  <span m="955040">S</span> <span m="955270">might</span> <span m="955510">be</span>
  <span m="955900">a</span> <span m="956170">value</span> <span m="956740">from</span>
  <span m="957010">1</span> <span m="957400">up</span> <span m="957610">to</span>
  <span m="958960">4,</span> <span m="959440">maybe</span> <span m="959710">1</span>
  <span m="959890">up</span> <span m="960010">to</span> <span m="960130">10</span>
  <span m="960910">where</span> <span m="961120">1</span> <span m="962290">is</span>
  <span m="962710">denoting</span> <span m="963250">a</span> <span m="964390">early</span>
  <span m="964780">disease</span> <span m="965080">stage</span> <span m="965680">and</span>
  <span m="966400">4 or</span> <span m="966775">10</span> <span m="967150">might</span>

  <span m="967990">later</span> <span m="968350">disease</span> <span m="968650">stage.</span>
  <span m="971430">If</span> <span m="971580">we</span> <span m="971700">have</span>
  <span m="971880">a</span> <span m="971940">sequence</span> <span m="972480">of</span>

  <span m="975540">observation</span> <span m="976110">on</span> <span m="976230">March</span>

  <span m="979380">disease</span> <span m="979620">stage</span> <span m="979980">by</span>

  <span m="981990">is</span> <span m="982050">going</span> <span m="982230">to</span>
  <span m="982350">talk</span> <span m="982680">about</span> <span m="983010">is</span>
  <span m="983220">the</span> <span m="983340">probability</span> <span m="983970">distribution</span>
  <span m="984480">of</span> <span m="984570">transitioning</span> <span m="985680">from</span>
  <span m="986010">whatever</span> <span m="986340">the</span> <span m="986430">disease</span>
  <span m="986670">stage</span> <span m="987060">at</span> <span m="987210">S1</span>
  <span m="987630">is</span> <span m="988170">to</span> <span m="988320">whatever</span>
  <span m="988560">the</span> <span m="988620">disease</span> <span m="988860">stage</span>
  <span m="989240">at</span> <span m="989490">S2.</span></p><p><span m="991200">Now</span>
  <span m="991380">because</span> <span m="991920">the</span> <span m="992100">time</span>
  <span m="992550">interval</span> <span m="992930">is</span> <span m="993060">between</span>

  <span m="1011220">the</span> <span m="1012990">transition</span> <span m="1013830">distribution--</span>

  <span m="1016380">of</span> <span m="1016530">transitioning</span> <span m="1017550">from</span>
  <span m="1018210">stage</span> <span m="1019020">I</span> <span m="1019560">at</span>
  <span m="1019740">time</span> <span m="1020130">t</span> <span m="1020340">minus</span>
  <span m="1020670">1</span> <span m="1021570">to</span> <span m="1021690">state</span>
  <span m="1022170">j</span> <span m="1022890">at</span> <span m="1023010">time</span>
  <span m="1023670">t,</span> <span m="1026710">given</span> <span m="1027250">as</span>
  <span m="1027490">input</span> <span m="1028420">the</span> <span m="1028869">difference</span>

  <span m="1031960">the</span> <span m="1032050">difference</span> <span m="1032470">in</span>
  <span m="1032560">time</span> <span m="1032859">points</span> <span m="1033540">delta--</span>
  <span m="1034060">so</span> <span m="1034210">delta</span> <span m="1034660">is</span>
  <span m="1035079">the</span> <span m="1035200">number</span> <span m="1035440">of</span>
  <span m="1035500">months</span> <span m="1035859">between</span> <span m="1036310">the</span>

  <span m="1040839">be</span> <span m="1040930">given</span> <span m="1041319">by</span>
  <span m="1042220">the</span> <span m="1042369">matrix</span> <span m="1043030">exponential</span>

  <span m="1048430">matrix</span> <span m="1048970">Q.</span></p><p><span m="1055560">And</span>
  <span m="1055650">then</span> <span m="1055890">here,</span> <span m="1056490">the</span>

  <span m="1199730">going</span> <span m="1199800">to</span> <span m="1199890">be</span>
  <span m="1199950">different</span> <span m="1200400">specifically</span> <span m="1200970">because</span>
  <span m="1201300">we</span> <span m="1201420">don't</span> <span m="1201600">know</span>
  <span m="1201750">the</span> <span m="1201840">time</span> <span m="1202140">intervals.</span>
  <span m="1203530">So</span> <span m="1203970">intuitively,</span> <span m="1204840">if</span>
  <span m="1205380">a</span> <span m="1205470">lot</span> <span m="1205800">of</span>

  <span m="1214110">different</span> <span m="1214410">stages</span> <span m="1215010">to</span>
  <span m="1215160">go</span> <span m="1215280">to</span> <span m="1215370">your</span>

  <span m="1216570">to</span> <span m="1216690">go</span> <span m="1216780">to</span>
  <span m="1216840">the</span> <span m="1216900">stage</span> <span m="1217140">of</span>

  <span m="1217570">step,</span> <span m="1217710">because</span> <span m="1217950">so</span>
  <span m="1218160">much</span> <span m="1218310">time</span> <span m="1218520">has</span>
  <span m="1218670">passed.</span></p><p><span m="1219800">And</span> <span m="1219900">that</span>

  <span m="3189120">is</span> <span m="3189240">diabetes,</span> <span m="3189870">in</span>
  <span m="3189960">black</span> <span m="3190320">here</span> <span m="3190470">is</span>

  <span m="3193590">disease.</span> <span m="3195300">And</span> <span m="3195400">so</span>

  <span m="3200300">even</span> <span m="3200780">in</span> <span m="3200900">stage</span>

  <span m="3224600">just</span> <span m="3224840">a</span> <span m="3225020">sanity</span>
  <span m="3225410">check</span> <span m="3225770">that</span> <span m="3226040">what</span>
  <span m="3226220">this</span> <span m="3226340">model</span> <span m="3226520">is</span>
  <span m="3226700">learning</span> <span m="3227540">for</span> <span m="3228200">a</span>
  <span m="3228290">common</span> <span m="3228830">disease</span> <span m="3229280">actually</span>
  <span m="3229610">aligns</span> <span m="3229910">with</span> <span m="3230010">the</span>

  <span m="3234560">I</span> <span m="3234620">want</span> <span m="3234770">to</span>
  <span m="3234890">say</span> <span m="3235160">about</span> <span m="3237590">this</span>
  <span m="3237800">probabilistic</span> <span m="3238340">model</span> <span m="3238970">approach</span>
  <span m="3239450">to</span> <span m="3239660">disease</span> <span m="3239990">progression</span>

  <span m="3241310">data.</span> <span m="3242060">I</span> <span m="3242090">want</span>
  <span m="3242240">you</span> <span m="3242300">to</span> <span m="3242360">hold</span>
  <span m="3242600">your</span> <span m="3242690">questions</span> <span m="3243560">so</span>
  <span m="3243710">I</span> <span m="3243800">can</span> <span m="3243920">get</span>
  <span m="3244130">through</span> <span m="3244340">the</span> <span m="3244400">rest</span>

  <span m="3245290">and</span> <span m="3245510">you</span> <span m="3245570">can</span>
  <span m="3245690">ask</span> <span m="3245840">me</span> <span m="3245900">after</span>
  <span m="3246110">class.</span> <span m="3247760">So</span> <span m="3248190">next</span>
  <span m="3248400">I</span> <span m="3248430">want</span> <span m="3248550">to</span>
  <span m="3248610">talk</span> <span m="3248820">about</span> <span m="3249330">these</span>
  <span m="3249630">pseudo-time</span> <span m="3250260">methods,</span> <span m="3250740">which</span>
  <span m="3250980">are</span> <span m="3251110">a</span> <span m="3251130">very</span>
  <span m="3251520">different</span> <span m="3251970">approach</span> <span m="3252510">for</span>
  <span m="3253170">trying</span> <span m="3253500">to</span> <span m="3253590">align</span>
  <span m="3253890">patients</span> <span m="3254250">into</span> <span m="3254460">early-to-late</span>
  <span m="3255120">disease</span> <span m="3255420">stage.</span> <span m="3257300">These</span>
  <span m="3257480">approaches</span> <span m="3257900">were</span> <span m="3258020">really</span>
  <span m="3258260">popularized</span> <span m="3258890">in</span> <span m="3258980">the</span>
  <span m="3259040">last</span> <span m="3259340">five</span> <span m="3259700">years</span>
  <span m="3260270">due</span> <span m="3260630">to</span> <span m="3261410">the</span>
  <span m="3262460">explosion</span> <span m="3263530">in</span> <span m="3263780">single-cell</span>
  <span m="3264680">sequencing</span> <span m="3265340">experiments</span> <span m="3265970">in</span>
  <span m="3266120">the</span> <span m="3266180">biology</span> <span m="3266640">community.</span></p><p><span
  m="3268660">Single-cell</span> <span m="3269160">sequencing</span> <span m="3269710">is</span>
  <span m="3269830">a</span> <span m="3269890">way</span> <span m="3270370">to</span>
  <span m="3270550">really</span> <span m="3270880">understand</span> <span m="3271900">not</span>

  <span m="3276850">a</span> <span m="3277690">cell-by-cell</span> <span m="3278680">basis</span>

  <span m="3280150">what</span> <span m="3280480">is</span> <span m="3280870">expressed</span>
  <span m="3281350">in</span> <span m="3281440">each</span> <span m="3281620">cell.</span>
  <span m="3283270">So</span> <span m="3283800">at</span> <span m="3283920">a</span>
  <span m="3283980">very</span> <span m="3284250">high</span> <span m="3284400">level,</span>
  <span m="3284780">the</span> <span m="3284850">way</span> <span m="3285000">this</span>
  <span m="3285180">works</span> <span m="3285600">is</span> <span m="3285690">you</span>
  <span m="3285780">take</span> <span m="3285990">a</span> <span m="3286050">solid</span>
  <span m="3286350">tissue,</span> <span m="3287370">you</span> <span m="3288570">do</span>
  <span m="3289080">a</span> <span m="3289170">number</span> <span m="3289930">of</span>
  <span m="3290620">procedures</span> <span m="3291270">in</span> <span m="3291350">order</span>
  <span m="3291600">to</span> <span m="3291780">isolate</span> <span m="3292290">out</span>
  <span m="3292470">individual</span> <span m="3293220">cells</span> <span m="3294090">from</span>
  <span m="3294600">that</span> <span m="3294810">tissue,</span> <span m="3295950">then</span>
  <span m="3296160">you're</span> <span m="3296280">going</span> <span m="3296670">to</span>
  <span m="3296880">extract</span> <span m="3297510">the</span> <span m="3297720">RNA</span>
  <span m="3298770">from</span> <span m="3299190">those</span> <span m="3299400">individual</span>
  <span m="3299760">cells,</span> <span m="3300960">you</span> <span m="3301440">go</span>
  <span m="3301710">through</span> <span m="3301890">another</span> <span m="3302220">complex</span>
  <span m="3302700">procedure</span> <span m="3303360">which</span> <span m="3304410">somehow</span>

  <span m="3309900">together,</span> <span m="3310920">does</span> <span m="3311130">sequencing</span>
  <span m="3311820">of</span> <span m="3311970">it,</span> <span m="3312180">and</span>
  <span m="3312300">then</span> <span m="3313290">deconvolves</span> <span m="3314070">it</span>

  <span m="3314520">can</span> <span m="3314640">see</span> <span m="3314880">what</span>

  <span m="3317070">RNA</span> <span m="3317610">expression</span> <span m="3318780">for</span>

  <span m="3319620">individual</span> <span m="3320070">cells.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="3339430">this</span> <span m="3339600">figure</span> <span m="3340090">part</span>

  <span m="3381350">differentiation?</span></p><p><span m="3382530">So</span> <span

  <span m="3383240">We</span> <span m="3383390">want</span> <span m="3383540">to</span>

  <span m="3403490">you</span> <span m="3403580">could</span> <span m="3403700">figure</span>

  m="3678420">So</span> <span m="3678580">there</span> <span m="3678700">are</span>
  <span m="3678730">a</span> <span m="3678790">variety</span> <span m="3679180">of</span>
  <span m="3679240">methods</span> <span m="3679810">to</span> <span m="3680950">try</span>
  <span m="3681130">to</span> <span m="3681250">infer</span> <span m="3682330">these</span>
  <span m="3682510">pseudo-times</span> <span m="3683110">under</span> <span m="3683350">a</span>
  <span m="3683470">variety</span> <span m="3683980">of</span> <span m="3684070">different</span>
  <span m="3684310">assumptions.</span> <span m="3685660">What</span> <span m="3685810">I'll</span>
  <span m="3685900">do</span> <span m="3686050">in</span> <span m="3686110">the</span>
  <span m="3686170">next</span> <span m="3686380">few</span> <span m="3686500">minutes</span>
  <span m="3686740">is</span> <span m="3686800">just</span> <span m="3686950">give</span>
  <span m="3687130">you</span> <span m="3687550">an</span> <span m="3687730">inkling</span>
  <span m="3688390">of</span> <span m="3688810">how</span> <span m="3689110">two</span>
  <span m="3689410">of</span> <span m="3689530">the</span> <span m="3689590">methods</span>
  <span m="3689950">work.</span> <span m="3691470">And</span> <span m="3691760">I</span>
  <span m="3691820">chose</span> <span m="3692060">these</span> <span m="3692240">to</span>
  <span m="3692330">be</span> <span m="3692420">representative</span> <span m="3693320">examples.</span>
  <span m="3695130">The</span> <span m="3695230">first</span> <span m="3695420">example</span>
  <span m="3696200">is</span> <span m="3697220">an</span> <span m="3697370">approach</span>
  <span m="3697850">based</span> <span m="3698330">on</span> <span m="3698690">building</span>
  <span m="3699290">a</span> <span m="3699590">minimum</span> <span m="3700130">spanning</span>
  <span m="3700610">tree.</span> <span m="3702530">And</span> <span m="3704060">this</span>
  <span m="3704210">algorithm</span> <span m="3704570">I'm</span> <span m="3704650">going</span>
  <span m="3704710">to</span> <span m="3704770">describe</span> <span m="3705140">goes</span>
  <span m="3705320">by</span> <span m="3705410">the</span> <span m="3705470">name</span>
  <span m="3705650">of</span> <span m="3705710">Monocle.</span> <span m="3706910">It</span>
  <span m="3707000">was</span> <span m="3707120">published</span> <span m="3707930">in</span>
  <span m="3708020">2014</span> <span m="3708960">in this</span> <span m="3709160">paper</span>
  <span m="3709430">by</span> <span m="3709610">Trapnell</span> <span m="3710030">et</span>
  <span m="3710120">al,</span> <span m="3710870">but</span> <span m="3711050">it</span>
  <span m="3711110">builds</span> <span m="3711500">very</span> <span m="3711860">heavily</span>
  <span m="3712400">on</span> <span m="3712550">an</span> <span m="3712670">earlier</span>
  <span m="3713060">published</span> <span m="3713750">paper</span> <span m="3714200">from</span>
  <span m="3714380">2003</span> <span m="3715220">that</span> <span m="3715340">I</span>
  <span m="3715410">mostly</span> <span m="3715620">citing</span> <span m="3715910">here.</span></p><p><span
  m="3718210">So</span> <span m="3718390">the</span> <span m="3718480">way</span>
  <span m="3718600">that</span> <span m="3718690">this</span> <span m="3718870">algorithm</span>
  <span m="3719230">works is</span> <span m="3719470">as</span> <span m="3719650">follows.</span>
  <span m="3720580">It</span> <span m="3720670">starts</span> <span m="3721570">with,</span>
  <span m="3722230">as</span> <span m="3723010">we've</span> <span m="3723190">been</span>
  <span m="3723340">assuming</span> <span m="3723670">all</span> <span m="3723760">along,</span>
  <span m="3724750">cross-sectional</span> <span m="3725530">data,</span> <span m="3725860">which</span>
  <span m="3726070">lives</span> <span m="3726310">in</span> <span m="3726400">some</span>
  <span m="3726610">high-dimensional</span> <span m="3727180">space.</span> <span
  m="3728140">I'm</span> <span m="3728260">drawing</span> <span m="3728560">that</span>
  <span m="3728710">in</span> <span m="3728800">the</span> <span m="3728860">top-left</span>
  <span m="3729730">here.</span> <span m="3730480">Each</span> <span m="3730750">data</span>
  <span m="3731080">point</span> <span m="3731800">corresponds</span> <span m="3732250">to</span>
  <span m="3732430">some</span> <span m="3733240">patient</span> <span m="3734500">or</span>
  <span m="3734620">some</span> <span m="3734830">cell.</span> <span m="3736450">The</span>
  <span m="3736540">first</span> <span m="3736870">step</span> <span m="3737080">of</span>
  <span m="3737140">the</span> <span m="3737200">algorithm</span> <span m="3737620">is</span>
  <span m="3737740">to</span> <span m="3737820">do</span> <span m="3737950">dimensionality</span>
  <span m="3738610">reduction.</span> <span m="3739270">And</span> <span m="3739730">there</span>
  <span m="3739830">are</span> <span m="3739930">many</span> <span m="3740030">ways</span>
  <span m="3740110">to</span> <span m="3740210">do</span> <span m="3740270">dimensionality</span>
  <span m="3740650">reduction.</span> <span m="3741010">You</span> <span m="3741100">could</span>
  <span m="3741250">do</span> <span m="3741490">principal</span> <span m="3741850">components</span>
  <span m="3742270">analysis,</span> <span m="3742900">or,</span> <span m="3743080">for</span>
  <span m="3743230">example,</span> <span m="3743650">you</span> <span m="3743740">could</span>
  <span m="3743890">do</span> <span m="3744010">independent</span> <span m="3744430">components</span>
  <span m="3744820">analysis.</span> <span m="3745570">This</span> <span m="3745750">paper</span>
  <span m="3745990">uses</span> <span m="3746170">the</span> <span m="3746260">independent</span>
  <span m="3746620">component</span> <span m="3746980">analysis.</span> <span m="3748240">What</span>
  <span m="3748450">ICA</span> <span m="3748810">is</span> <span m="3748900">going</span>
  <span m="3749010">to</span> <span m="3749080">do,</span> <span m="3749230">it's</span>
  <span m="3749330">going to</span> <span m="3749440">attempt</span> <span m="3749710">to</span>
  <span m="3749800">find</span> <span m="3750010">a</span> <span m="3750040">number</span>
  <span m="3750340">of</span> <span m="3750400">different</span> <span m="3750670">components</span>
  <span m="3751150">that</span> <span m="3751270">seem</span> <span m="3751510">to</span>
  <span m="3751570">be</span> <span m="3751660">as</span> <span m="3751810">independent</span>
  <span m="3752290">from</span> <span m="3752470">one</span> <span m="3752590">another</span>
  <span m="3752830">as</span> <span m="3752950">possible.</span></p><p><span m="3755260">Then</span>
  <span m="3755410">you're</span> <span m="3755500">going</span> <span m="3755650">to</span>
  <span m="3755770">represent</span> <span m="3756460">the</span> <span m="3756610">data</span>
  <span m="3757030">now</span> <span m="3757420">in</span> <span m="3757570">this</span>
  <span m="3757780">low-dimensional</span> <span m="3758440">space,</span> <span m="3759400">and</span>
  <span m="3759910">in</span> <span m="3760180">many</span> <span m="3760570">of</span>
  <span m="3760630">these</span> <span m="3760780">papers,</span> <span m="3761140">it's</span>
  <span m="3761260">quite</span> <span m="3761470">astonishing</span> <span m="3761890">to</span>
  <span m="3762040">me,</span> <span m="3762250">they</span> <span m="3762400">actually</span>
  <span m="3762670">use</span> <span m="3762910">dimension</span> <span m="3763390">2.</span>
  <span m="3764660">So</span> <span m="3764780">they'll</span> <span m="3764930">go</span>
  <span m="3765140">all</span> <span m="3765470">the</span> <span m="3765530">way</span>
  <span m="3765620">down</span> <span m="3765770">to</span> <span m="3765830">two-dimensional</span>
  <span m="3766370">space</span> <span m="3766620">where</span> <span m="3766710">you</span>
  <span m="3766760">can</span> <span m="3766880">actually</span> <span m="3767150">plot</span>
  <span m="3767465">all</span> <span m="3767780">of</span> <span m="3767960">the</span>
  <span m="3768050">data.</span> <span m="3770260">It's</span> <span m="3770310">not</span>
  <span m="3770580">at</span> <span m="3770670">all</span> <span m="3770790">obvious</span>
  <span m="3771030">to</span> <span m="3771090">me</span> <span m="3771180">why</span>
  <span m="3771360">you</span> <span m="3771420">would</span> <span m="3771510">want</span>
  <span m="3771660">to</span> <span m="3771720">do</span> <span m="3771810">that,</span>
  <span m="3771990">and</span> <span m="3772110">for</span> <span m="3772230">clinical</span>
  <span m="3772620">data,</span> <span m="3772870">I</span> <span m="3772950">think</span>
  <span m="3773160">that</span> <span m="3773280">might</span> <span m="3773460">be</span>
  <span m="3773580">a</span> <span m="3773640">very</span> <span m="3773820">poor</span>
  <span m="3774060">choice.</span> <span m="3776610">Then</span> <span m="3777090">what</span>
  <span m="3777270">they</span> <span m="3777390">do</span> <span m="3777660">is</span>
  <span m="3777870">they</span> <span m="3778080">build</span> <span m="3779010">a</span>
  <span m="3779100">minimum</span> <span m="3779490">spanning</span> <span m="3780120">tree</span>
  <span m="3781140">on</span> <span m="3781740">all</span> <span m="3782070">of</span>
  <span m="3782160">the</span> <span m="3782250">patient</span> <span m="3782700">or</span>
  <span m="3782760">cells.</span></p><p><span m="3784920">So</span> <span m="3785100">the</span>
  <span m="3785190">way</span> <span m="3785340">that</span> <span m="3785490">one</span>
  <span m="3785730">does</span> <span m="3786030">that</span> <span m="3786390">is</span>
  <span m="3786570">you</span> <span m="3786750">create</span> <span m="3787230">a</span>
  <span m="3787320">graph</span> <span m="3788490">by</span> <span m="3788700">drawing</span>
  <span m="3789240">an</span> <span m="3789480">edge</span> <span m="3789840">between</span>
  <span m="3790380">every</span> <span m="3790710">pair</span> <span m="3791220">of</span>
  <span m="3791370">nodes</span> <span m="3792420">where</span> <span m="3792600">the</span>
  <span m="3792720">weight</span> <span m="3793230">of</span> <span m="3793410">the</span>
  <span m="3793530">edge</span> <span m="3794070">is</span> <span m="3794280">the</span>
  <span m="3794370">Euclidean</span> <span m="3795030">distance</span> <span m="3795690">between</span>
  <span m="3796140">those</span> <span m="3796380">two</span> <span m="3797340">points.</span>
  <span m="3800130">And</span> <span m="3800280">then--</span> <span m="3800700">so</span>
  <span m="3800850">for</span> <span m="3800940">example,</span> <span m="3801340">there</span>
  <span m="3801420">is</span> <span m="3801750">this</span> <span m="3802020">edge</span>
  <span m="3802290">from</span> <span m="3802500">here</span> <span m="3802770">to</span>
  <span m="3802860">here,</span> <span m="3803190">there's</span> <span m="3803320">an</span>
  <span m="3803430">edge</span> <span m="3803640">from</span> <span m="3803850">here</span>
  <span m="3804030">to</span> <span m="3804150">here</span> <span m="3804420">and</span>
  <span m="3804510">so</span> <span m="3804750">on.</span> <span m="3806130">And</span>
  <span m="3806220">then</span> <span m="3806430">given</span> <span m="3806760">that</span>
  <span m="3806940">weighted</span> <span m="3807810">graph,</span> <span m="3808740">we're</span>
  <span m="3808830">going</span> <span m="3808980">to</span> <span m="3809100">find</span>
  <span m="3809520">the</span> <span m="3809640">minimum</span> <span m="3810090">spanning</span>
  <span m="3810510">tree</span> <span m="3810690">of</span> <span m="3810750">that</span>
  <span m="3810900">graph,</span> <span m="3812050">and</span> <span m="3812070">what</span>
  <span m="3812190">I'm</span> <span m="3812310">showing</span> <span m="3812670">you</span>
  <span m="3812820">here</span> <span m="3813330">is</span> <span m="3813660">the</span>
  <span m="3813780">minimum</span> <span m="3814080">spanning</span> <span m="3814410">tree</span>
  <span m="3814590">of</span> <span m="3814650">the</span> <span m="3814740">corresponding</span>
  <span m="3815130">graph,</span> <span m="3815925">OK?</span></p><p><span m="3818100">Next,</span>
  <span m="3818330">what</span> <span m="3818480">one</span> <span m="3818690">will</span>
  <span m="3818840">do</span> <span m="3819350">is</span> <span m="3819500">go</span>
  <span m="3819670">look</span> <span m="3819920">for</span> <span m="3820100">the</span>
  <span m="3820220">longest</span> <span m="3821090">path</span> <span m="3822020">in</span>
  <span m="3822200">that</span> <span m="3822710">tree.</span> <span m="3825440">Remember,</span>
  <span m="3826160">finding</span> <span m="3826520">the</span> <span m="3826610">longest</span>
  <span m="3827210">path</span> <span m="3827750">in</span> <span m="3827900">a</span>
  <span m="3827960">graph--</span> <span m="3828670">in</span> <span m="3828770">an</span>
  <span m="3828890">arbitrary</span> <span m="3829310">graph</span> <span m="3829880">has</span>
  <span m="3830120">a</span> <span m="3830180">name,</span> <span m="3830610">it's</span>
  <span m="3830630">called</span> <span m="3830960">the</span> <span m="3831830">traveling</span>
  <span m="3832310">salesman</span> <span m="3832700">problem</span> <span m="3833030">and</span>
  <span m="3833120">it's</span> <span m="3833210">the</span> <span m="3833270">NP-hard</span>
  <span m="3833750">problem.</span> <span m="3835170">How</span> <span m="3835330">has</span>
  <span m="3835450">that</span> <span m="3835510">gotten</span> <span m="3835730">around</span>
  <span m="3835960">here?</span> <span m="3836230">Well</span> <span m="3836350">we're</span>
  <span m="3836470">not--</span> <span m="3836710">this</span> <span m="3836860">is</span>
  <span m="3836930">not</span> <span m="3837040">an</span> <span m="3837130">arbitrary</span>
  <span m="3837550">graph,</span> <span m="3837910">this</span> <span m="3838090">is</span>
  <span m="3838210">actually</span> <span m="3838860">a</span> <span m="3840280">tree.</span>
  <span m="3841190">So</span> <span m="3842440">here's</span> <span m="3842720">that</span>
  <span m="3842830">poor--</span> <span m="3843460">here's</span> <span m="3843850">a</span>
  <span m="3843910">algorithm</span> <span m="3844630">for</span> <span m="3844810">finding</span>
  <span m="3845110">the</span> <span m="3845170">longest</span> <span m="3846760">path.</span>
  <span m="3848420">I</span> <span m="3848470">won't</span> <span m="3848610">talk</span>
  <span m="3848770">about</span> <span m="3848890">that.</span></p><p><span m="3851360">So</span>
  <span m="3852260">one</span> <span m="3852470">finds</span> <span m="3852890">along</span>
  <span m="3853190">this</span> <span m="3853340">path</span> <span m="3853910">in</span>
  <span m="3854150">a</span> <span m="3854210">tree--</span> <span m="3854990">in</span>
  <span m="3855410">the</span> <span m="3855470">tree,</span> <span m="3856220">and</span>
  <span m="3856340">then</span> <span m="3856550">what</span> <span m="3856700">one</span>
  <span m="3856910">does</span> <span m="3857210">is</span> <span m="3857300">one</span>
  <span m="3857510">says,</span> <span m="3857820">OK,</span> <span m="3858230">one</span>
  <span m="3858590">side</span> <span m="3858950">of</span> <span m="3859010">the</span>
  <span m="3859100">path</span> <span m="3860390">corresponds</span> <span m="3861080">to,</span>
  <span m="3861200">let's</span> <span m="3861350">say,</span> <span m="3861560">early</span>
  <span m="3861980">disease</span> <span m="3862340">stage</span> <span m="3862790">and</span>
  <span m="3862880">the</span> <span m="3862940">other</span> <span m="3863120">side</span>
  <span m="3863300">of</span> <span m="3863360">the</span> <span m="3863430">path</span>
  <span m="3863750">corresponds</span> <span m="3864170">to</span> <span m="3864260">late</span>
  <span m="3864470">disease</span> <span m="3864740">stage,</span> <span m="3866270">and</span>
  <span m="3866480">it</span> <span m="3866570">allows</span> <span m="3866870">for</span>
  <span m="3866960">the</span> <span m="3867050">fact</span> <span m="3867290">that</span>
  <span m="3867380">there</span> <span m="3867500">might</span> <span m="3867620">be</span>
  <span m="3867740">some</span> <span m="3867980">bifurcation.</span> <span m="3868820">So</span>
  <span m="3869120">for</span> <span m="3869210">example,</span> <span m="3869570">you</span>
  <span m="3869690">see</span> <span m="3869840">here</span> <span m="3870110">that</span>
  <span m="3870290">there</span> <span m="3870480">is</span> <span m="3870750">a</span>
  <span m="3870920">bifurcation</span> <span m="3871730">over</span> <span m="3871970">here.</span>
  <span m="3873530">And</span> <span m="3873830">as</span> <span m="3874010">we</span>
  <span m="3874100">discussed</span> <span m="3874490">earlier,</span> <span m="3874980">you</span>
  <span m="3875080">have</span> <span m="3875120">to</span> <span m="3875240">have</span>
  <span m="3875450">some</span> <span m="3875720">way</span> <span m="3875870">of</span>
  <span m="3875960">differentiating</span> <span m="3877280">what</span> <span m="3877760">the</span>
  <span m="3877880">beginning</span> <span m="3878300">is</span> <span m="3878430">and</span>
  <span m="3878490">what</span> <span m="3878600">the</span> <span m="3878690">end</span>
  <span m="3878870">should</span> <span m="3878990">be,</span> <span m="3879200">and</span>
  <span m="3879290">that's</span> <span m="3879530">where</span> <span m="3879740">some</span>
  <span m="3879920">side</span> <span m="3880130">information</span> <span m="3880520">might</span>
  <span m="3880610">become</span> <span m="3880880">useful.</span></p><p><span m="3883280">So</span>
  <span m="3883400">here's</span> <span m="3883640">an</span> <span m="3883970">illustration</span>
  <span m="3884570">of</span> <span m="3884720">applying</span> <span m="3885170">that</span>
  <span m="3885320">method</span> <span m="3885590">to</span> <span m="3885680">some</span>
  <span m="3885830">real</span> <span m="3886010">data.</span> <span m="3887490">So</span>
  <span m="3888260">every</span> <span m="3888500">point</span> <span m="3888890">here</span>
  <span m="3889280">is</span> <span m="3890210">a</span> <span m="3890810">cell</span>
  <span m="3891710">after</span> <span m="3892160">doing</span> <span m="3892640">dimensionality</span>
  <span m="3893090">reduction.</span> <span m="3894200">The</span> <span m="3894590">edges</span>
  <span m="3895010">between</span> <span m="3895400">those</span> <span m="3895610">points</span>
  <span m="3896000">correspond</span> <span m="3896510">to</span> <span m="3896630">the</span>
  <span m="3896750">edges</span> <span m="3897200">of</span> <span m="3897440">the</span>

  <span m="4128410">is a</span> <span m="4128479">way</span> <span m="4128620">to</span>
  <span m="4128710">get</span> <span m="4128830">a</span> <span m="4128890">distribution</span>
  <span m="4129700">over</span> <span m="4130000">functions</span> <span m="4130810">just</span>
  <span m="4130990">by</span> <span m="4131109">sampling</span> <span m="4131740">from</span>
  <span m="4131950">this</span> <span m="4132130">Gaussian</span> <span m="4132670">process.</span></p><p><span
  m="4135130">What</span> <span m="4135310">this</span> <span m="4135490">paper</span>
